## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the population growth rate dP/dt as a function of time t and population P, which is the fundamental problem of population dynamics. The relationship likely involves density-dependent growth terms where growth rate depends nonlinearly on current population size.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (density-independent unlimited growth)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (growth rate decreasing logarithmically with population)
- Theta-logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with nonlinear density dependence)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P * c1 - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth negative at low and high densities)
- Allee effect (weak): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (c2 + P) (reduced but positive growth at low density)
- Von Bertalanffy-type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolic vs catabolic scaling)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (flexible sigmoidal growth)
- Time-varying logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) + c2 * t * P (logistic with time-dependent component)
- Polynomial density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (cubic population dynamics)
- Oscillatory carrying capacity: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t))) (seasonal environment)
- Power-law growth with saturation: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 / (1 + c2 * P) (growth with resource limitation)
- Delayed density dependence proxy: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) + c2 * t (time as proxy for lagged effects)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope â†’ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects â†’ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay â†’ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior â†’ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects â†’ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent per-capita growth rate declining linearly with P â†’ logistic form: dP/dt = r*P*(1 - P/K), i.e., quadratic in P
- Cubic terms in P (PÂ³) â†’ Allee effects or bistability in population dynamics, indicating multiple equilibria
- Logarithmic dependence on P (log(P)) â†’ Gompertz-type growth where per-capita rate decreases logarithmically
- Fractional power of P (P^c where 0<c<1) â†’ metabolic scaling or surface-area-limited resource uptake
- Product of P with trigonometric function of t â†’ seasonal or periodic environmental forcing on population growth
- Ratio of polynomials in P â†’ functional response-type saturation in self-limitation (e.g., P/(1+P) terms)
- Multiple roots in the growth rate function (factored polynomial in P) â†’ multiple equilibrium points with distinct stability
- Time appearing only through slow polynomial drift (e.g., c*t) â†’ gradually changing environmental conditions or carrying capacity
